<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div>


<p align="center" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:center;text-indent:0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">SCHEDULE
TO</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This Tender Offer Statement on Schedule TO relates to
an offer (the &#147;<b>Offer</b>&#148;) by Apple Inc., a
California corporation (&#147;<b>Apple</b>&#148; or the &#147;<b>Company</b>&#148;), to amend certain options (the &#147;<b>Eligible Options</b>&#148;) that have been granted under the Company&#146;s
1997 Employee Stock Option Plan (the &#147;<b>Plan</b>&#148;): (i)
that had original exercise prices per share that were less than the fair market
value per share of the common stock underlying the option on the date that the
grant was finalized, (ii) that were unvested, either in whole or in part, as of
December 31, 2004, (iii) that are outstanding as of the last date on which the
Offer remains open for acceptance, and (iv)&nbsp;that are held by individuals
who are subject to taxation in the United States.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Eligible participants may elect to (i) amend Eligible
Options to increase the exercise price per share to the fair market value of a
share of the Company&#146;s common stock on the option&#146;s grant date of record (the &#147;<b>New Exercise Price</b>&#148;), and (ii) for each amended Eligible
Option, receive a cash payment equal to the difference between the New Exercise
Price and the original exercise price per share.&#160; Cash payments will be paid on or promptly
following January 25, 2008, and all such payments will be subject to any
applicable tax withholding.&#160; Cash
payments will not be subject to any further vesting conditions and will be made
without regard to whether the Eligible Option is vested and whether an eligible
participant is an employee or other service provider of the Company.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The amendment of the Eligible Options will be made
pursuant to the terms and subject to the conditions set forth in: (i) the Offer
to Amend the Exercise Price of Certain Options, dated March 16, 2007 (the &#147;<b>Offer to Amend</b>&#148;), (ii) the Email to All Eligible Option
Holders, (iii) the Election Form, and (iv) the Withdrawal Form.&#160; These documents, as they may be amended or
supplemented from time to time, together constitute the &#147;<b>Offer
Documents</b>&#148; and are attached to this Schedule TO as Exhibits
(a)(1)(A) through (a)(1)(D), respectively.&#160;
An &#147;<b>Eligible Option Holder</b>&#148; refers to
an individual who holds Eligible Options to purchase shares of Apple common
stock that are outstanding on the last date on which this offer remains open
for acceptance and who is subject to taxation in the United States.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This Offer is being made upon the terms and subject to
the conditions set forth in the Offer to Amend, which, as may be amended or
supplemented from time to time, constitutes the Offer, and which is filed as
Exhibit (a)(1)(A) hereto.&#160; This Tender
Offer Statement on Schedule TO is intended to satisfy the reporting
requirements of Section 13(e) of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as
amended.&#160; The information in the Offer
Documents, including all schedules and annexes to the Offer Documents, is incorporated
by reference in answer to the items required in this Schedule TO.</font></p>

<h1 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Item 1. Summary Term Sheet.</font></b></h1>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The information set forth under the caption &#147;Summary
Term Sheet and Questions and Answers&#148; in the Offer to Amend is incorporated
herein by reference.</font></p>

<h1 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Item 2. Subject Company Information.</font></b></h1>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <b><i style="font-weight:bold;">Name and Address.</i></b></font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Apple Inc. is the issuer of the securities subject to
the Offer to Amend.&#160; The address of the
Company&#146;s principal executive office is 1 Infinite Loop, Cupertino,
California&#160; 95014 and the telephone
number at that address is (408) 996-1010.&#160;
The information set forth in the Offer to Amend in the section under the
caption &#147;The Offer&#148; entitled &#147;Information concerning the Company&#148; is
incorporated herein by reference.</font></p>


 <p style="margin:24.0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2</font></p> <br><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="center">

<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='2',FILE='C:\fc\741573286_D11431_1873176\8219-1-da.htm',USER='jmsproofassembler',CD='Mar 15 15:07 2007' -->
<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">



<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <b><i style="font-weight:bold;">Securities.</i></b></font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This Tender Offer Statement on Schedule TO relates to
an offer by the Company to holders of Eligible Options granted under&nbsp;the
Plan to amend such Eligible Options and to receive a cash payment with respect
to each amended Eligible Option, as set forth in the Offer to Amend and upon
the terms and subject to the conditions described in (i) the Offer to Amend
attached hereto as Exhibit&nbsp;(a)(1)(A), (ii) the Email to All Eligible
Option Holders attached hereto as Exhibit (a)(1)(B), (iii) the Election Form
attached hereto as Exhibit (a)(1)(C), and (iv) the Withdrawal Form attached
hereto as Exhibit (a)(1)(D).</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As of March 13, 2007, there were options to purchase
114,695 shares of the Company&#146;s common stock outstanding and eligible to
participate in this Offer.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(c)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <b><i style="font-weight:bold;">Trading Market and Price.</i></b></font></p>

  (incorporated herein by reference to Exhibit 4.11 to Registration Statement

<p align="right" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:right;text-indent:36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Exhibit (a)(1)(A)</font></b></p>

<p align="right" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:right;text-indent:36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p align="right" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:right;text-indent:36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p align="right" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:right;text-indent:36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p align="right" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:right;text-indent:36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p align="right" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:right;text-indent:36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p align="right" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:right;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="line-height:9.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">

<hr size="1" width="160" noshade color="black" align="center" style="width:120.0pt;">

</font></b></div>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">APPLE INC.</font></b></p>

<div style="line-height:9.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">

<hr size="1" width="160" noshade color="black" align="center" style="width:120.0pt;">

</font></b></div>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">OFFER TO AMEND THE EXERCISE PRICE
OF CERTAIN OPTIONS</font></b></p>

<div style="line-height:9.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:center;"><hr size="1" width="160" noshade color="black" align="center" style="width:120.0pt;"></div>

<p align="center" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:center;text-indent:0pt;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">This
document constitutes part of the prospectus relating to the Apple Inc. 1997
Employee Stock Option Plan covering securities that have been registered under
the Securities Act of 1933, as amended.</font></i></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:center;text-indent:0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">March 16,
2007</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

</div><br><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="center">

<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='',FILE='C:\fc\7442649269_H10188_1869683\8219-1-ka.htm',USER='jmsproofassembler',CD='Mar 15 04:26 2007' -->



<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div>


<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">APPLE INC.</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Offer to Amend the Exercise Price
of Certain Options</font></b></p>

<div style="line-height:9.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:center;"><hr size="1" width="160" noshade color="black" align="center" style="width:120.0pt;"></div>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">This offer and withdrawal rights
will expire at<br>
5:00 p.m., Pacific Time, on Monday, April 16, 2007 unless we extend them.</font></b></p>

<div style="line-height:9.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:center;"><hr size="1" width="160" noshade color="black" align="center" style="width:120.0pt;"></div>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">By this Offer to Amend the Exercise Price of Certain
Options (the &#147;Offer to Amend&#148;), we are giving all eligible option holders
holding eligible options to purchase shares of our common stock the right to
amend certain outstanding options and to receive cash payments for such amended
eligible options (we refer to this as the &#147;offer&#148;). Each eligible option holder
who has eligible options outstanding is being provided with an addendum
(referred to as the &#147;Addendum&#148;) setting forth his or her eligible options, the
new exercise price that would apply to each eligible option (if amended) and a
description of the cash payments for such eligible options, and other relevant
information.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">It has been determined that certain of your stock
options were erroneously assigned grant dates that preceded the finalization of
those grants.&#160; As a result, the exercise
prices of these stock options were lower than they would have been if the
options had been dated when the grants were actually finalized, and therefore
may be subject to adverse tax consequences under Section 409A of the United States
Internal Revenue Code of 1986, as amended (the &#147;Internal Revenue Code&#148;). These
consequences include taxable ordinary income recognition in the year of
vesting, an additional 20% penalty tax and interest charges. If you elect to
participate in this offer, your eligible options should no longer be subject to
the adverse tax consequences under Section 409A.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">You are an &#147;eligible option holder&#148; only if you are
(1) subject to taxation in the United States and (2) hold eligible options to
purchase common stock of Apple Inc. that are outstanding on the last date on
which this offer remains open for acceptance. You do not need to be an active
employee of Apple Inc. or our subsidiaries (collectively referred to as &#147;Apple,&#148;
the &#147;Company,&#148; &#147;we,&#148; &#147;our&#148; or &#147;us&#148;) in order to be an eligible option holder.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">An option to purchase Apple common stock is eligible
for this offer (an &#147;eligible option&#148;) only if each of the following conditions
is met:</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>the
option was granted under Apple&#146;s 1997 Employee Stock Option Plan (the &#147;Plan&#148;);</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>the
option had an original exercise price per share that was less than the fair
market value per share of the common stock underlying the option on the date
the grant was actually finalized;</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>the
option was unvested as of December 31, 2004 (if only a portion of an option was
unvested as of December 31, 2004, the unvested portion of the option may be an &#147;eligible
option&#148;); and</p>


 <p style="margin:24.0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">1</font></p> <br><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="center">

<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='1',FILE='C:\fc\74103731106_H10187_1871385\8219-1-kc.htm',USER='jmsproofassembler',CD='Mar 15 10:37 2007' -->
<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">



<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>the
option is outstanding as of the last date on which this offer remains open for
acceptance.</p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">If you participate in this offer, then for each
eligible option for which you accept this offer, the following will occur:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">1.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Your
eligible options will be amended to increase the exercise price per share to
the fair market value of a share of Apple&#146;s common stock on the date that Apple
determined that the grant was actually finalized (the &#147;new exercise price&#148;). If
only a portion of your option was unvested as of December 31, 2004, then only
that portion of the option is an eligible option and will be amended to
increase the exercise price. Your Addendum lists the original exercise price of
your eligible options (referred to as the &#147;original exercise price&#148;), as well
as the new exercise price of such options, should you accept this offer in
connection with those options; and</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; For
each such eligible option amended in this offer, you will receive, on or
promptly following January 25, 2008, a cash payment equal to the difference
between the new exercise price of the amended option and the original exercise
price, multiplied by the number of unexercised shares of Apple&#146;s common stock
subject to the eligible option that was amended in the manner described below.
Your Addendum lists the number of unexercised shares subject to your eligible
options and the cash payment you will be entitled to receive for each eligible
option you elect to have amended.</font></p>

<h1 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Receipt of Amended Options and Cash
Payments</font></i></h1>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">If you elect to receive an amended option for an
eligible option, the eligible option will be amended on the date that this
offer expires (but following the expiration of the offer), which is currently
expected to be Monday, April 16, 2007 at 5:00 p.m., Pacific Time). Promptly
following the expiration of the offer, you will receive a document entitled &#147;Amendment(s)
to Stock Option Agreements and Promise to Make Cash Payment&#148; evidencing the
amendment of the options you elected to amend. Each amended option will be
subject to the terms and conditions of the Plan and as amended in accordance
with this offer. Any amended option you receive will continue to be subject to
the same vesting schedule.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In addition, the &#147;Amendment(s) to Stock Option
Agreements and Promise to Make Cash Payment&#148; will evidence your right to
receive a cash payment for the eligible options you elected to have amended.
Cash payments will be paid on or promptly following January 25, 2008, and all
such payments will be subject to any applicable tax withholding. Cash payments
will not be subject to any further vesting conditions, so you will receive any
cash payments to which you are entitled on or promptly following January 25,
2008, regardless of whether the eligible option is vested and regardless of
whether you are employed with us at that time.</font></p>

<h1 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Other Matters</font></i></h1>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The offer is not conditioned upon its acceptance by a
minimum number of participants or outstanding eligible options, but the offer
is subject to the conditions that we describe in Section 7 of this Offer to
Amend, &#147;Conditions of the offer&#148;. You are not required to accept this offer.</font></p>


 <p style="margin:24.0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2</font></p> <br><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="center">

<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='2',FILE='C:\fc\74103731106_H10187_1871385\8219-1-kc.htm',USER='jmsproofassembler',CD='Mar 15 10:37 2007' -->
<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">



<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Our common stock is traded on the NASDAQ Global Select
Market under the symbol &#147;AAPL.&#148;&#160; On March
13, 2007, the closing price of our common stock was $88.40<b>  </b>per
share as reported on the NASDAQ Global Select Market. You should evaluate
current market quotes for our common stock, among other factors, before deciding
to participate in this offer.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">See &#147;Risks of Participating in the Offer&#148;
beginning on page 15 for a discussion of risks that you should consider before
participating in this offer.</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">IMPORTANT&#151; STEPS YOU MUST TAKE TO
PARTICIPATE</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">If you participate in this offer, you must complete
and sign the attached election form, and fax it to (408) 253-7457 before 5:00
p.m., Pacific Time, on Monday, April 16, 2007. Only responses that are
completed, signed, and actually received via fax by Apple by the deadline will
be accepted. Responses may be submitted only via fax. Responses submitted by
any other means, including email, hand delivery, United States mail (or other
post) and Federal Express (or similar delivery service), are not permitted.
Responses that are received after the deadline will not be accepted. The
delivery of election and withdrawal forms is at your risk. Apple intends to
confirm the receipt of your election form and/or any withdrawal form by email
within two U.S. business days. If you have not received an email confirmation
that Apple has received your response, we recommend that you confirm that we
have received your election form and/or any withdrawal form. If you need to
confirm receipt after two U.S. business days have elapsed, you may email stockquestions@apple.com
or contact Sheri Parker at 408-974-2683.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Neither the Securities and Exchange Commission (the &#147;SEC&#148;)
nor any state securities commission has approved or disapproved of these
securities or passed upon the accuracy or adequacy of this offer. Any
representation to the contrary is a criminal offense.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Apple will provide general tax information to eligible
option holders regarding this offer. Apple will not provide tax advice specific
to an individual&#146;s circumstances or make any tax recommendation. We recommend
that you discuss the personal tax consequences of this offer with your
financial, legal and/or tax advisors. If you have general questions about the
terms of this offer or requests for general tax information about this offer
you may email stockquestions@apple.com or contact Sheri Parker at<br>
408-974-2683.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Offer to Amend the Exercise Price
of Certain Options, dated March 16, 2007.</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">You should rely only on the information contained
in this Offer to Amend or documents to which we have referred you. We have not
authorized anyone to provide you with different information. In addition, some
states, including California, may impose additional penalty taxes. We recommend
that you consult with your financial, legal and/or tax advisors regarding any tax
consequences, including any state tax consequences. Although our board of
directors has approved this offer, neither we nor our board of directors make
any recommendation as to whether you should accept this offer. The decision to
participate in the offer must be your own, after taking into account your
personal circumstances and preferences. We are not making an offer of the cash
consideration or amended options in any jurisdiction in which the offer is not
permitted. We are not aware of any jurisdiction where the making of the offer
is not in compliance </font></b></p>


 <p style="margin:24.0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3</font></p> <br><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="center">

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">with applicable law. If we become
aware of any jurisdiction where the making of the offer is not in compliance
with any valid applicable law, we will make a good faith effort to comply with
such law. If, after such good faith effort, we cannot comply with such law, the
offer will not be made to, nor will options be accepted from the option holders
residing in such jurisdiction. The information provided in this Offer to Amend
is accurate only as of the date such information is shown, or if no date is
indicated, the date of this offer.</font></b></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div>


<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Q1.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; What is the offer?</font></b></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A1.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>This
offer is a voluntary opportunity for eligible option holders to elect to have
certain outstanding options amended and, for such amended options, receive a
cash payment. This opportunity is described in the following questions and
answers, and in the remainder of this Offer to Amend.</p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Terms Used in the Offer</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The following are some terms that are frequently used
in this Offer to Amend.</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>&#147;original
exercise price&#148; refers to the original exercise price of an eligible option, as
described in Question and Answer 7. Your Addendum lists the original exercise
price of each of your eligible options.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>&#147;amended
options&#148; refers to eligible options that are amended pursuant to this offer.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>&#147;amendment
date and time&#148; refers to the date and time when the eligible options for which
you accept this offer will be amended to reflect the new exercise price. We
expect that the amendment date and time will be Monday, April 16, 2007, on the
same date as, but at a later time than, the expiration of the offer. If the
expiration of the offer is extended, then the amendment date and time will be
similarly changed to the new date of the expiration of the offer.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>&#147;Addendum&#148;
refers to the document that is being provided to each eligible option holder.
The Addendum lists eligible options and, for each eligible option, lists the
original exercise price, the number of unexercised shares subject to the
eligible option, the new exercise price if the option is amended and the cash
payment related to the eligible option if it is amended.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>&#147;directors
and executive officers&#148; refers to those directors and officers of Apple listed
on Schedule A, including those who are officers for purposes of Section 16 of
the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the &#147;Exchange Act&#148;). None of
our directors or executive officers holds eligible options and therefore none
of our directors or executive officers is an eligible option holder.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>&#147;eligible
option holder&#148; refers to all individuals who (1) are subject to United States
taxation and (2) hold eligible options, if those options are outstanding as of
the last date on which this offer remains open for acceptance.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>&#147;eligible
options&#148; refers to options that satisfy each of the conditions described in
Question and Answer 4. You may accept this offer to amend eligible options and
receive cash payments, as described in Question and Answer 4 and Section 1 of
this Offer to Amend.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>&#147;expiration
of the offer&#148; refers to the date and time that this offer expires. The
expiration of the offer will occur at 5:00 p.m., Pacific Time, on Monday, April
16, 2007,</p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">unless the offer
is extended. We may extend the expiration of the offer at our discretion. If we
extend the offer, the term &#147;expiration of the offer&#148; will refer to the date and
time at which the extended offer expires.</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>&#147;new

may be exercised to purchase Apple common stock. An amended option&#146;s new
exercise price will be equal to the fair market value of a share of Apple
common stock on the date that Apple determined the grant was actually
finalized. Your Addendum lists the new exercise price for each of your eligible
options should you accept this offer to amend such options.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>&#147;offer
period&#148; or &#147;offering period&#148; refers to the period from the commencement of this
offer to the expiration of the offer. This period will commence on March 16,
2007, and end at 5:00 p.m., Pacific Time, on Monday, April 16, 2007, unless the
offer is extended.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>&#147;Plan&#148;
refers to Apple&#146;s 1997 Employee Stock Option Plan.</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>&#147;Section
409A&#148; refers to Section 409A of the United States Internal Revenue Code of
1986, as amended, and the proposed tax regulations thereunder.&#160; Section 409A was enacted under the American
Jobs Creation Act of 2004 (see page 35 under the subsection entitled &#147;Uncertainty,&#148;
for a discussion of the uncertainty caused by the fact that the tax regulations
are proposed and not final).</p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Q2.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Why is Apple making this offer?</font></b></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A2.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>It
has been determined that certain of your stock options were erroneously
assigned grant dates that preceded the finalization of those grants.&#160; As a result, the exercise prices of these
stock options were lower than they would have been if the options had been
dated when the grants were actually finalized, and therefore may be subject to
adverse tax consequences under Section 409A of the United States Internal
Revenue Code of 1986, as amended (the &#147;Internal Revenue Code&#148;). These
consequences include taxable ordinary income recognition in the year of
vesting, an additional 20% penalty tax and interest charges. If you elect to
participate in this offer, your eligible options should no longer be subject to
the adverse tax consequences under Section 409A, as described in Section 14 of
this Offer to Amend. (See Section 3)</p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Q3.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Who is eligible to participate in this
offer?</font></b></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A3.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>You
may participate in this offer if you (1) are subject to United States taxation
and (2) hold eligible options, if those options are outstanding as of the last
date on which this offer remains open for acceptance.</p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">You do not need to be an
active employee of Apple in order to be an eligible option holder. However, if
you are no longer an active employee of Apple, your options will have ceased to
vest in accordance with their terms and you will be eligible to participate in
this offer only if you hold eligible options which have vested and are
outstanding as of the last date on which this offer remains open for
acceptance. (See Section 1)</font></p>


 <p style="margin:24.0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2</font></p> <br><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="center">

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">None of our directors or
executive officers holds eligible options and therefore none of our directors
or executive officers is eligible to participate in this offer. (See Section 1)</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Q4.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Which options are eligible for
amendment in this offer?</font></b></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A4.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>An
option to purchase common stock is an eligible option under this offer only if
each of the following conditions is met:</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>the
option was granted under the Plan;</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>the
option had an original exercise price per share that was less than the fair
market value per share of the common stock underlying the option on the date
the grant was actually finalized;</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>the
option was unvested as of December 31, 2004 (if only a portion of an option was
unvested as of December 31, 2004, the unvested portion may be an &#147;eligible
option&#148;); and</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>the
option is outstanding as of the last date on which this offer remains open for
acceptance.</p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Q5.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; How do I participate in this offer?</font></b></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A5.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>If
you choose to participate in this offer, you must do the following before 5:00
p.m., Pacific Time, on Monday, April 16, 2007 (which we refer to as the &#147;expiration
of the offer&#148;):</p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">1.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Properly
complete and sign the attached election form; and</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Fax
the completed and signed election form to (408) 253-7457.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">If you participate in
this offer, you will be required to accept the offer for the entire eligible
portion of each eligible option you elect to amend. In other words, you must
accept the offer for all the shares subject to a particular eligible option,
but not necessarily for all your eligible options, if you hold more than one
eligible option. To help you determine your outstanding eligible options, we
are providing you with an Addendum listing your eligible options, the new
exercise price that will apply if the eligible options are amended and the cash
payment you will receive for the eligible options, if amended. If you hold an
option that is not listed on the Addendum, the option is not an eligible
option.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This is a one-time offer,
and we will strictly enforce the election period. We reserve the right to
reject any election related to options for which you have elected to accept
this offer that we determine are not eligible or that we determine are not
permissible to accept. Subject to the terms and conditions of this offer, we
will accept all eligible options for which a proper election has been made
promptly after the expiration of this offer. (See Section 4)</font></p>

election form and/or any withdrawal form. If you need to confirm receipt after

contact Sheri Parker at 408-974-2683. Responses may only be submitted via fax.

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Q6.</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>If
I decide to participate in the offer, what will happen to my current eligible
options?</b></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A6.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>If
you elect to participate in the offer, your eligible options will be amended on
the amendment date and time, on the same date as, but following the time of,
the expiration of the offer. The expiration of the offer will take place on
Monday, April 16, 2007, unless the offer period is extended. In addition, if
you elect to participate in this offer, you will become entitled to receive the
cash payment described below, less any applicable tax withholding.</p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The amended option will
continue to be subject to the terms and conditions of the Plan, as amended in
accordance with this offer. (See Section 6)</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Q7.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; What will I receive in return for my
options?</font></b></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A7.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>If
you participate in this offer, then for each eligible option for which you
accept this offer, the following will occur:</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">1.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Your
eligible options will be amended to increase the exercise price per share to
the new exercise price. The new exercise price will be the fair market value of
a share of Apple common stock on the date that Apple determined the grant was
actually finalized.</p>


 <p style="margin:24.0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">4</font></p> <br><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="center">

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">



<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">If only a portion of your
option was unvested as of December 31, 2004, then only that portion of the
option is an eligible option and will be amended to increase the exercise
price. The portion that vested on or before December 31, 2004 is not subject to
the adverse tax consequences that this offer is designed to allow you to avoid
and so that portion of the option will not be eligible for inclusion in the
offer. Instead, the portion of any option that vested on or before December 31,
2004 will remain outstanding in accordance with its original terms, including
its adjusted original exercise price.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Your Addendum lists the
adjusted original exercise price of your eligible options, as well as the new
exercise price of such options, should you accept this offer to amend those
options.</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>In
addition, you will receive, on or promptly following January 25, 2008, a cash
payment equal to the difference between the new exercise price of the amended
option and the original exercise price multiplied by the number of shares
corresponding to the unexercised portion of the eligible option that was
amended, in the manner described below.</p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Your Addendum lists the
number of shares corresponding to the unexercised portion of your eligible
options and the cash payment you will be entitled to receive for each eligible
option you elect to have amended. Note that your cash payment is subject to any
applicable tax withholding.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For purposes of this
offer, the term &#147;option&#148; generally refers to an option to purchase one or more
shares of our common stock.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:0pt;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Eligible
Option Example</font></i></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">You were issued an option to purchase 1,000 shares of
Apple common stock with an exercise price equal to $25.00 per share (this is
the option&#146;s original exercise price). Of the number of shares subject to your
eligible option, 250 shares vested on or before December 31, 2004. On the date
the grant was actually finalized, the fair market value of Apple common stock
was $26.00 per share. As of the expiration of the offer, you had not exercised
any portion of the option. Since the option&#146;s original exercise price of $25.00
is less than $26.00, the option will be an eligible option for 750 shares (the
250 shares that vested on or before December 31, 2004 are not subject to
Section 409A and are therefore not eligible). If you properly accept this offer
to amend that option, the following will occur:</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">1.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The
option to purchase 750 shares will be amended to increase the exercise price to
$26.00 per share; and</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>A
cash payment of $750.00 ($26.00-$25.00 multiplied by 750 shares) (the portion
of the option eligible as of the expiration of the offer), less any applicable
tax withholding, will be payable to you on or promptly following January 25,
2008.</p>


 <p style="margin:24.0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">5</font></p> <br><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="center">

<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='5',FILE='C:\fc\74162528581_D11851_1873766\8219-1-ki.htm',USER='jmsproofassembler',CD='Mar 15 16:25 2007' -->
<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">



<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Q8.</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>When
will I receive my amended options and cash payments?</b></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A8.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Any
eligible options for which you have elected to accept this offer will be
amended on the amendment date and time, on the same date as, but following the
time of, the expiration of the offer. The amendment date and time will be the
same date as, but following the time of, the expiration of the offer. We currently
expect that the expiration of the offer and the amendment date and time will be
Monday, April 16, 2007. If the expiration of the offer is delayed, the
amendment date and time will be similarly delayed. Promptly after the
expiration of the offer, you will receive an &#147;Amendment(s) to Stock Option
Agreements and Promise to Make Cash Payment&#148; evidencing the amendment of the
options you elected to amend. (See Section 6)</p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In addition, the &#147;Amendment(s)
to Stock Option Agreements and Promise to Make Cash Payment&#148; will evidence your
right to receive a cash payment for the eligible options you elected to have
amended. Any cash payment owed to you will be paid to you, less any applicable
tax withholding, on or promptly following January 25, 2008. This payment will
not be subject to any vesting conditions or otherwise be subject to forfeiture.
(See Section 6)</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Q9.</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Why
won&#146;t I receive my cash payment immediately following the expiration of the
offer?</b></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A9.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The
proposed tax regulations under Section 409A that allow us to offer you the
opportunity to avoid unfavorable tax consequences by amending your options also
impose certain requirements regarding the timing of the cash payments. These
proposed tax regulations do not allow us to make the cash payments in the same
calendar year in which the options are amended. Therefore, the earliest we can
make these cash payments to eligible option holders who participate in the
offer is January 25, 2008, the earliest date for which we pay for services
rendered to us exclusively in 2008.&#160; Any
cash payments received for eligible options that you elect to amend will be
subject to regular income and employment tax withholding at the time of
receipt.</p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Q10.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Am I required to participate in this
offer?</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A10.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; No.&#160; Participation in this offer is completely
voluntary.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">However, if you do
participate in this offer, for each eligible option that you elect to have
amended in this offer, you must accept this offer to amend the entire
outstanding portion of that option, to the extent that it was unvested as of
December 31, 2004 and except as described in Question and Answer 35. (See
Section 2)</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">If you do not participate
in this offer, you may be subject to certain adverse tax consequences. Please
also see Questions and Answers 15 and 16 for a description of the potential tax
consequences to you if you decide not to participate in the offer and instead
keep your current options.</font></p>


 <p style="margin:24.0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">6</font></p> <br><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="center">

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Q11.</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Once
my election has been accepted, is there anything I must do to receive the
amended options or cash payments?</b></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A11.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Once your
election has been accepted, there is nothing that you must do to receive your
amended options. Your amended options will be amended on the amendment date and
time, on the same date as, but following the time of, the expiration of the
offer. (See Section 2)</p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">You also do not need to
do anything in order to receive your cash payments for the eligible options.
Note that you will receive a cash payment only regarding your eligible options
that are amended in this offer. The cash payment for these options, less any
applicable tax withholding, will be made on or promptly following January 25,
2008. Promptly following the expiration of the offer, we will send you an &#147;Amendment(s)
to Stock Option Agreements and Promise to Make Cash Payment&#148; evidencing your
right to receive a cash payment for these options. This payment will not be
subject to any vesting conditions or otherwise be subject to forfeiture.</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Q12.</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Will
the terms and conditions of my amended options be the same as my original
options?</b></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A12.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Yes. Except
for the new exercise price of your amended options, the terms and conditions of
your amended options will remain the same as the terms and conditions of your
eligible options. (See Sections 2, 9 and 14)</p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Q13.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; When will my amended options vest?</font></b></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A13.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>If your options
are amended, they will continue to vest according to the vesting schedule of
your original options. Future vesting is subject to your continued employment
with us through each relevant vesting date. (See Section 9)</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Q14.</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>What
happens to my options if I elect to participate in the offer to amend eligible
options but then exercise those options before expiration of the offer?</b></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A14.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>If you
elect to participate in the offer but exercise your eligible options prior to
expiration of the offer, those options which you exercise will no longer be
eligible to be amended in this offer and you will not receive a cash payment
for such options. Your options instead will terminate when you exercise those
options, in accordance with their terms. (See Question and Answer 15) In
addition, for those eligible options you exercise prior to expiration of the
offer, you may be required to recognize taxable ordinary income and may also be
subject to an additional 20% penalty tax plus an interest charge under Section
409A.</p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Furthermore, some states,
including California, may impose additional penalty taxes on the amounts
subject to the 20% federal penalty tax. (See Section 14)</font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div>


<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Q15.</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>What
happens to my options if I do not turn in my election form by the deadline,
choose not to participate or my options are not accepted?</b></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A15.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>If we do
not receive your properly completed election form by the deadline, you choose
not to participate, or your options are not accepted by us under this offer,
your existing options will (1) remain outstanding until they expire by their
terms, including but not limited to expiration in connection with your
termination of employment, (2) retain their original exercise price, (3) retain
their share amount available for purchase, (4) retain their current terms for
exercise, and (5) retain their current vesting schedule. As described in
Question and Answer 2, you may be required to recognize ordinary income before
the options are exercised and may also be subject to an additional 20% penalty
tax plus an interest charge under Section 409A. In addition, some states,
including California, may impose additional penalty taxes on the amounts
subject to the 20% federal penalty tax. We recommend that you consult with your
financial, legal and/or tax advisors regarding any tax consequences, including
any state tax consequences. (See Section 14)</p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Q16.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; What are the tax consequences if I
participate in the offer?</font></b></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A16.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>As a result
of participation in this offer, you may avoid potentially adverse tax
consequences associated with your eligible options under United States tax law.</p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Section 409A and proposed
tax regulations under the American Jobs Creation Act of 2004 provide that stock
options granted with an exercise price lower than the fair market value of the
underlying stock on the date the grant was actually finalized must have fixed
exercise dates to avoid early income recognition and an additional 20% tax.
None of the eligible options have fixed exercise dates, and therefore Section
409A would likely subject the eligible option holders to income recognition
before the options are exercised and would subject the eligible option holders
to the additional 20% tax.&#160; The Internal
Revenue Service has not issued final guidance with respect to the taxation of
such misdated options under Section 409A. It is likely that the eligible option
holders would have income recognition equal to the difference between the fair
market value of the shares on the date of vesting and the exercise price (the &#147;spread&#148;).&#160; The eligible option holders would incur an
additional 20% penalty tax on the income recognized, plus possibly an interest
charge.&#160; Further, it is possible that
during each subsequent tax year (until the option is exercised), the increase
in value of the underlying stock will be subject to taxable income recognition.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Apple cannot guarantee
any particular tax results related to your options; furthermore, there is
uncertainty because the proposed tax regulations are not final. However, Apple
will withhold taxes and report income amounts to the IRS and other taxing
authorities as required by applicable laws. Because this offer involves complex
tax considerations, we urge you to consult your financial, legal and/or tax
advisor before you make any decisions about participating in this offer.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Please also see Question
and Answer 15 for a description of the potential consequences to you if you
decide not to participate in the offer and instead keep your current options.</font></p>


 <p style="margin:24.0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">8</font></p> <br><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="center">

<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='8',FILE='C:\fc\7444855156_H10188_1869751\8219-1-kk.htm',USER='jmsproofassembler',CD='Mar 15 04:49 2007' -->
<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">



<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">If you participate in the
offer, you should not be required under current United States law to recognize
income for United States federal income tax purposes on the option at the time
you choose to accept the offer. On the amendment date and time, you should not
be required under current law to recognize income for United States federal
income tax purposes for any amended options. However, you will have taxable
income for the cash payments you receive for eligible options that are amended.
(See Section 14) In addition, you may have taxable income when you exercise
your amended options or when you sell your shares. (See Section 14)</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:0pt;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Uncertainty</font></i></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Unfortunately, the
Internal Revenue Service (the &#147;IRS&#148;) has only issued proposed regulations and
has not issued definitive final guidance under Section 409A. It is possible
that final guidance issued by the IRS may differ from our current good-faith
interpretation of the law and that you and your personal tax advisor may
advocate a position under the current statute and IRS guidance that your
eligible options are exempt from Section 409A. We cannot guarantee the effect
of any future IRS guidance and will work as quickly as practicable when future
guidance is issued to analyze it and provide any new information to our
eligible option holders regarding such guidance.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In addition, if you are
subject to taxation in the United States, and also are subject to taxation in
another country, there may be additional tax consequences relating to your
participation in this offer. <b><i style="font-weight:bold;">Further, some states,
including California, may impose additional penalty taxes on the amounts
subject to the 20% federal penalty tax. We recommend that you consult with your
financial, legal and/or tax advisors regarding any tax consequences, including
any state tax consequences.</i></b></font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Q17.</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>If
I choose to participate in this offer, are there circumstances under which my
eligible options would be amended but I would not receive a cash payment for
them?</b></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A17.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>No.
However, your option will not be amended and cash payment will not be made if
we are prohibited from doing so by applicable laws or rules. For example, we
could become prohibited from amending options as a result of changes in SEC,
National Association of Securities Dealers or NASDAQ Global Select Market
rules. We do not anticipate any such prohibitions at this time. (See Section
13)</p>

options under the terms of the Plan. Therefore, if your employment with Apple
terminates after your eligible options are amended pursuant to this offer, your
amended eligible options will cease to vest in accordance with their terms.
However, if you elect to participate in this offer prior to the termination of
your </p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">own. <b><i style="font-weight:bold;">We
