<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">If You Do Not Participate in this Offer.</font></i></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The following is a summary of the material United
States federal income tax consequences of declining to participate in the offer
for those eligible option holders subject to United States federal income tax.
This discussion is based on the United States Internal Revenue Code, its
legislative history, treasury proposed tax regulations thereunder and administrative
and judicial interpretations as of the date of this Offer to Amend, all of
which are subject to change, possibly on a retroactive basis. The federal tax
laws may change and the federal, state and local tax consequences for each
eligible option holder will depend upon that eligible option holder&#146;s
individual circumstances. This summary does not discuss all of the tax
consequences that may be relevant to you in light of your particular
circumstances, nor is it intended to be applicable in all respects to all
categories of option holders. If you are subject to taxation in the United
States, and are also subject to the tax laws of another country, you should be
aware that there might be other tax and social security consequences that may
apply to you. In addition, some states, including California, may impose
additional penalty taxes on the amounts subject to the 20% federal penalty tax.
We strongly recommend that you consult with your own advisors to discuss the
consequences to you of this transaction.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">We strongly recommend that you
consult your financial, legal and/or tax advisors regarding the federal, state
and local tax consequences of participating in the offer, as the tax
consequences to you are dependent on your individual tax situation. If you have
general questions regarding the terms of this offer or requests for general tax
information about this offer please email stockquestions@apple.com or contact
Sheri Parker at 408-974-2683.</font></i></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Your decision not to accept this offer for your
eligible options could result in potentially adverse tax consequences to you.
Please read this section carefully and talk to your tax advisors about your
decision regarding participation in this offer.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Section 409A and proposed tax regulations under the
American Jobs Creation Act of 2004 provide that stock options granted with an
exercise price lower than the fair market value of the underlying stock on the
date the grant was actually finalized must have fixed exercise dates to avoid
early income recognition and an additional 20% tax. None of the eligible
options have fixed exercise dates and therefore they may subject the eligible
option holders to income recognition before the options are exercised and would
subject the eligible option holders to the additional 20% penalty tax on the
income recognized, plus possibly an interest charge. Further, it is possible
that during each subsequent tax year (until the option is exercised), the
increase in value of the underlying stock will be taxed and may also be subject
to the additional 20% penalty tax on the income recognized and a potential
interest charge.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:0pt;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Uncertainty</font></i></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Unfortunately, the Internal Revenue Service (the &#147;IRS&#148;)
has not issued definitive final guidance under Section 409A. It is possible
that final guidance issued by the IRS may differ from our current good-faith
interpretation of the law and that you and your personal tax advisor may
advocate a position under the current statute and IRS guidance that your
eligible options are exempt from Section 409A. We cannot guarantee the effect
of any future IRS guidance and will work as quickly as practicable when future
guidance is issued to analyze it and provide information to our eligible option
holders regarding such guidance.</font></p>

<h2 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">15.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Extension of offer; termination;
amendment.</font></b></h2>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We reserve the right, at our discretion, at any time
and regardless of whether or not any event listed in Section 7 of this Offer to
Amend has occurred or is deemed by us to have occurred, to extend the period of
time during which the offer is open and delay the acceptance for amendment of
any options. If we elect to extend the period of time during which this offer
is open, we will give you written notice of the extension and delay, as
described below. If we extend the expiration of the offer, we will also extend
your right to withdraw elections for eligible options until the new date of the
expiration of the offer. In the case of an extension, we will issue an email or
other form of communication no later than 6:00 a.m., Pacific Time, on the next
U.S. business day after the previously scheduled expiration of the offer.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We also reserve the right, in our reasonable judgment,
before the expiration of the offer to terminate or amend the offer and to
postpone the expiration of the offer (resulting in a delay of our acceptance
and amendment of any options for which elections have been made) if any of the
events listed in Section 7 of this Offer to Amend occurs, by giving written
notice of the termination or postponement to you or by making a public
announcement of the termination. Our reservation of the right to delay our
acceptance and amendment of options for which elections have been made is
limited by Rule 13e-4(f)(5) under the Exchange Act which requires that we must
pay the consideration offered or return the options promptly after termination
or withdrawal of an offer like this.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Subject to compliance with applicable law, we further
reserve the right, before the expiration of the offer, in our discretion, and
regardless of whether any event listed in Section 7 of this Offer to Amend has
occurred or is deemed by us to have occurred, to amend the offer in any
respect, including by decreasing or increasing the consideration offered in this
offer to option holders or by decreasing or increasing the number of options
being sought in this offer. As a reminder, if a particular option expires after
commencement, but before amendment under the offer, that particular option is
not eligible for amendment. Therefore, if we extend the offer for any reason
and if a particular option for which an election to accept the offer was made
before the originally scheduled expiration of the offer expires after such
originally scheduled expiration of the offer but before the actual amendment
date and time under the extended offer, that option would not be eligible for
amendment.</font></p>


 <p style="margin:24.0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">36</font></p> <br><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="center">

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The minimum period during which the offer will remain
open following material changes in the terms of the offer or in the information
concerning the offer, other than a change in the consideration being offered by
us or a change in amount of existing options sought, will depend on the facts
and circumstances of such change, including the relative materiality of the
terms or information changes. If we modify the number of eligible options being
sought in this offer or the consideration being offered by us for the eligible
options in this offer, the offer will remain open for at least ten U.S.
business days from the date of notice of such modification. If any term of the
offer is amended in a manner that we determine constitutes a material change
adversely affecting any holder of eligible options, we will promptly disclose
the amendments in a manner reasonably calculated to inform holders of eligible
options of such amendment, and we will extend the offer&#146;s period so that at
least five U.S. business days, or such longer period as may be required by the
tender offer rules, remain after such change.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For purposes of the offer, a &#147;business day&#148; means any
day other than a Saturday, Sunday or a United States federal holiday and
consists of the time period from 12:01 a.m. through 12:00 midnight, U.S.
Eastern Time.</font></p>

<h2 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">16.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Fees and expenses.</font></b></h2>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We will not pay any fees or commissions to any broker,
dealer or other person for soliciting elections for this offer.</font></p>

<h2 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">17.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Additional information.</font></b></h2>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This Offer to Amend is part of a Tender Offer
Statement on Schedule TO that we have filed with the SEC. This Offer to Amend
does not contain all of the information contained in the Schedule TO and the
exhibits to the Schedule TO. We recommend that you review the Schedule TO,
including its exhibits, and the following materials that we have filed with the
SEC before making a decision on whether to elect to accept this offer for your
options:</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">1.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Our
annual report on Form 10-K for our fiscal year ended September 30, 2006, filed
with the SEC on December 29, 2006;</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Our

of shareholders, filed with the SEC on March 14, 2006;</p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Our
quarterly report on Form 10-Q for our fiscal quarter ended December 30, 2006

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">4.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Our
current reports on Form 8-K as filed with the SEC on January 10, 2007 and

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">5.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The

551-8090. Our SEC filings are also available to the public on the SEC&#146;s

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Each person to whom a copy of this Offer to Amend is

emailing stockquestions@apple.com or contacting Sheri Parker at 408-974-2683.</font></p>

<h2 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">18.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Financial statements.</font></b></h2>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Attached as Schedule B to this Offer to Amend is our
summary financial information for our annual report on Form 10-K for our fiscal

fiscal quarter ended December 30, 2006. More complete financial information may
be obtained by accessing our public filings with the SEC by following the
instructions in Section 17 of this Offer to Amend.</font></p>

<h2 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;page-break-after:avoid;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">19.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Miscellaneous.</font></b></h2>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We are not aware of any jurisdiction where the making
of the offer is not in compliance with applicable law. If we become aware of
any jurisdiction where the making of the offer is not in compliance with any
valid applicable law, we will make a good faith effort to comply with such law.
If, after such good faith effort, we cannot comply with such law, the offer
will not be made to, nor will options be accepted from the option holders
residing in such jurisdiction.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">We have not authorized any person
to make any recommendation on our behalf as to whether you should elect to
accept this offer to amend your options. Apple will prepare communications
regarding this offer and provide general tax information to eligible option
holders regarding this offer. Apple will not provide tax advice specific to an
individual&#146;s circumstances or make any tax recommendation. You should rely only
on the information in this document or documents to which we have referred you.
We have not authorized anyone to give you any information or to make any
representations in connection with the offer other than the information and
representations contained in this Offer to Amend the Exercise Price of Certain
Options and in the related offer documents. If anyone makes any recommendation
or representation to you or gives you any information, you must not rely upon
that recommendation, representation or information as having been authorized by
us.</font></i></b></p>

<head>







</head>

<body lang="EN-US">

<div>


<p align="right" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:right;text-indent:36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Exhibit (a)(1)(B)</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:24.0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">DRAFT EMAIL TO ALL ELIGIBLE OPTION HOLDERS</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:24.0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">To:&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; [EMAIL ADDRESS]</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">From:&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; stockquestions@apple.com</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Date:&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; March 16, 2007</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Subject:&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Action Required: Urgent
Information Regarding Your Unexercised Stock Options</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This email contains important information about your
unexercised stock options.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As you may know, Apple recently announced that certain
stock option grants made to employees between 1997 and 2002 were erroneously
assigned grant dates that preceded the finalization of those grants.&#160; As a result, the exercise prices of these
stock option grants were lower than they would have been if the grants had been
dated when they were actually finalized.&#160;
Some misdated stock options exercised after 2005 are now subject to
additional taxes, including an additional 20% tax and interest, under Section
409A of the Internal Revenue Code.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Our records indicate that some of your Apple stock
options will fall into this category if you exercise them in the future. These
options are listed in the attached Addendum.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">To help you avoid Section 409A charges, Apple is
offering to amend the strike price on your misdated stock options. This would
raise the strike price on these options to reflect the price that would have
existed if the grants had been dated when they were actually finalized. Apple
will then issue you a cash payment to make up for the difference between the
new strike price and the price at which you were originally granted the stock
options.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Participation in this offer is completely voluntary.
Changing the strike price requires a &#147;Tender Offer&#148; to you from Apple, which is
included with this letter. Cash payments will be paid on or promptly following
January 25, 2008, and will be subject to normal tax withholdings. The remaining
terms and conditions of your stock options will remain unchanged.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">It is extremely important that you carefully review
the documents attached to this letter, as they contain the information that you
need in order to decide whether or not to participate in this offer.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">DOCUMENTS AND MATERIALS</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(1)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Tender
Offer Document</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">[TENDER OFFER DOCUMENT ATTACHED]</font></p>


<br><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="center">

<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='',FILE='C:\fc\7452336809_H10188_1869943\8219-1-kw.htm',USER='jmsproofassembler',CD='Mar 15 05:23 2007' -->
<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">



<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(2)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Election
Form:</p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">[ELECTION FORM ATTACHED]</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(3)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Withdrawal
Form:</p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">[WITHDRAWAL FORM ATTACHED]</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 36.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(4)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Addendum
to the Tender Offer with your personalized stock option information (includes a
list of your &#147;eligible&#148; option grants, the originally assigned grant date of
each of those options, the amended option exercise price, and a description of
cash payments if you choose to participate in the Tender Offer):</p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">[ADDENDUM ATTACHED]</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">After reviewing these materials, if you wish to
participate in the Tender Offer, you will need to fill out, sign and date the
attached Election Form. The Election Form must be received by Apple via fax at
(408) 253-7457 no later than 5:00 p.m., Pacific Time, on Monday, April 16, 2007.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">We encourage you to discuss the
personal tax consequences of this offer with your financial, legal and/or tax
advisors before deciding whether or not to participate in this offer.</font></i></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We apologize for any inconvenience or confusion this
situation may have caused. If you have any questions, please email
stockquestions@apple.com or call Sheri Parker at 408-974-2683.</font></p>

<p align="right" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:right;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Exhibit
(a)(1)(C)</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">APPLE INC.<br>
<br>
OFFER TO AMEND THE EXERCISE PRICE OF CERTAIN OPTIONS<br>
<u>ELECTION FORM</u></font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Before signing this
election form, please make sure you received, read and understand the documents
that make up this offer, including:&#160; (1)
the Offer to Amend the Exercise Price of Certain Options (the &#147;Offer to Amend&#148;);
(2) the Email to All Eligible Option Holders; (3) this Election Form; (4) and
the Withdrawal Form.&#160; The offer is
subject to the terms of these documents as they may be amended.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The offer provides
eligible option holders who hold eligible options the opportunity to (i) amend
certain outstanding and unexercised options, and (ii) receive a cash payment
for such amended options, as described in Section 2 of the Offer to Amend.&#160; This offer expires at 5:00 p.m., Pacific
Time, on Monday, April 16, 2007, unless extended.&#160; PLEASE FOLLOW THE INSTRUCTIONS ATTACHED TO
THIS FORM.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">If you participate in
this offer, you will be required to accept the offer for the entire eligible
portion of each eligible option you elect to amend. In other words, you must
accept the offer for all the shares subject to a particular eligible option,
but not necessarily for all your eligible options, if you hold more than one
eligible option.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:center;text-indent:0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">BY PARTICIPATING, YOU AGREE TO ALL TERMS OF THE<br>
OFFER AS SET FORTH IN THE OFFER DOCUMENTS.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">If you would like to
participate in this offer, please indicate your election by checking the box
below and completing and signing this election form.&#160; Please be sure to follow the instructions,
which are attached.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">You may withdraw this election as to some or all of
your options by submitting a properly completed and signed withdrawal form
prior to the expiration of the offer, which will be 5:00 p.m., Pacific Time,
Monday, April 16, 2007, unless extended.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Please check the
appropriate box:</font></p>

grants listed on the Addendum issued to me.</b></p>

 <p style="margin:24.0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2</font></p> <br><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="center">

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">APPLE INC.</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">OFFER TO AMEND THE EXERCISE PRICE
OF CERTAIN OPTIONS<br>
ELECTION FORM INSTRUCTIONS</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">FORMING PART OF THE TERMS AND
CONDITIONS OF THE OFFER</font></b></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-72.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">1.</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Delivery
of Election Form.</b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A properly completed and
signed election form must be received by the Company via facsimile at (408)
253-7457 on or before 5:00 p.m., Pacific Time, on Monday, April 16, 2007
(referred to as the expiration of the offer).</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">The
delivery of all required documents, including election forms, is at your
risk.&#160; Delivery will be deemed made only
when actually received via fax by the Company.&#160;
You should allow sufficient time to ensure timely delivery.&#160; Apple intends to confirm the receipt of your
election form by email within two U.S. business days.&#160; If you have not received such an email
confirmation, it is your responsibility to ensure that your election form has
been received by 5:00 p.m., Pacific Time, on Monday, April 16, 2007.&#160; Only responses that are complete, signed and
actually received by the Company by the deadline will be accepted.&#160; Responses may only be submitted via fax.&#160; Responses submitted by any other means,
including hand delivery, email, United States mail (or other post) and Federal
Express (or similar delivery service), are not permitted.</font></i></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Apple&#146;s receipt of your
election form is not by itself an acceptance of your options for
amendment.&#160; For purposes of the offer, we
will be deemed to have accepted options for amendment for which valid elections
have been made and not properly withdrawn as of when we give oral or written
notice to the option holders generally of our acceptance of such options.&#160; We may issue this notice of acceptance by
press release, email or other methods of communication.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Apple will not accept any
alternative, conditional or contingent elections.&#160; Although it is Apple&#146;s intent to send you an
email confirmation of receipt of this election form, by signing this election
form, you waive any right to receive any notice of the receipt of the election
to amend your options, except as provided for in the Offer to Amend.&#160; Any confirmation of receipt sent to you will
merely be a notification that the Company has received your election form and
does not mean that your options have been amended.&#160; Your options that are accepted will be
amended on the same day as, but at a later time than, the expiration of the
offer.&#160; The expiration of the offer is expected
to be 5:00 p.m., Pacific Time, Monday, April 16, 2007 (but following the
expiration of the offer).</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-72.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">2.</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Withdrawal.</b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">If you have previously elected to accept this offer to
amend your eligible options, you may withdraw that election for some or all of
these options at any time before the expiration of the offer, which is expected
to be 5:00 p.m., Pacific Time, on Monday, April 16, 2007. If we extend the
offer, you may withdraw your election for some or all of your eligible options
at any time until the date and time of the extended expiration of the offer.</font></p>


 <p style="margin:24.0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3</font></p> <br><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="center">

<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='3',FILE='C:\fc\7410308857_H10187_1871385\8219-1-ky.htm',USER='jmsproofassembler',CD='Mar 15 10:30 2007' -->
<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">



<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In addition, although we intend to accept, promptly
after the expiration of this offer, all valid elections, if we have not
accepted your election by 5:00 p.m., Pacific Time on Wednesday, April 18, 2007,
you may withdraw your election at any time thereafter.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">To validly withdraw an earlier election, you must fax
to (408) 253-7457, in accordance with the procedures listed in Section 4 above,
a signed and dated withdrawal form with the required information, while you
still have the right to withdraw the election for those options. Any election
you do not withdraw will remain effective pursuant to your prior election form.
You may change your mind as many times as you wish, but you will be bound by
the last properly submitted election or withdrawal form we receive before the
expiration of the offer. Apple must receive the properly completed and signed
withdrawal form before the expiration date. The expiration of the offer will be
5:00 p.m., Pacific Time, on Monday, April 16, 2007, unless we extend the offer.</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-72.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">3.</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Elections.</b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">If you participate in this offer, you will be required
to accept the offer for the entire eligible portion of each eligible option you
elect to amend. In other words, you must accept the offer for all the shares
subject to a particular eligible option, but not necessarily for all your
eligible options, if you hold more than one eligible option. If you have
exercised a portion of an eligible option grant, your election will apply to
the portion that remains outstanding and unexercised.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">If you have an eligible option grant that is subject
to a domestic relations order (or comparable legal document as the result of
the end of a marriage) and a person who is not an eligible option holder
beneficially owns a portion of that option grant, you may accept this offer for
the entire remaining outstanding portion of the option if so directed by the
beneficial owner as to his or her portion in accordance with the applicable
domestic relations order or comparable legal documents. As legal owner of the
eligible option, Apple will respect an election properly made by you and
accepted by Apple and will not be responsible to you or the beneficial owner of
the eligible option for any errors made by you in such an election.</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-72.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">4.</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Signatures
on this Election Form.</b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">If this election form is
signed by the holder of the options, the signature must correspond with the
name as written on the face of the option agreement or agreements to which the
options are subject without alteration, enlargement or any change whatsoever.&#160; If your name has been legally changed since
your option agreement was signed, please submit proof of the legal name change.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">If this election form is
signed by a trustee, executor, administrator, guardian, attorney-in-fact,
officer of a corporation or other person acting in a fiduciary or
representative capacity, that person should so indicate when signing, and
proper evidence satisfactory to Apple of the authority of that person to act in
that capacity must be submitted with this election form.</font></p>


 <p style="margin:24.0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">4</font></p> <br><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="center">

<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='4',FILE='C:\fc\7410308857_H10187_1871385\8219-1-ky.htm',USER='jmsproofassembler',CD='Mar 15 10:30 2007' -->
<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">



<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-72.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">5.</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Other
Information on This Election Form.</b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In addition to signing this election form, you must
print your name and employee number, if any, and indicate the date and time at
which you signed.&#160; You must also include
your current corporate email address, or, if no current corporate email address
is applicable, then a current email address at which you can be contacted.</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-72.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">6.</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Requests
for Assistance or Additional Copies.</b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">You should direct general
questions about the terms of this offer, requests for general tax information
about this election form or any requests for additional copies of this Offer to
Amend about this offer to stockquestions@apple.com or contact Sheri Parker at
408-974-2683.&#160; Copies will be furnished
promptly at Apple&#146;s expense.</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-72.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">7.</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Irregularities.</b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We will determine, in our
discretion, all questions as to the validity, form, eligibility (including time
of receipt) and acceptance of any options.&#160;
Our determination of these matters will be final and binding on all
parties.&#160; We reserve the right to reject
any election form or any options for which elections have been made that we
determine are not in good order or that we determine are unlawful to
accept.&#160; We will accept all options for
which proper elections are made that are not validly withdrawn.&#160; We also reserve the right to waive any of the
conditions of the offer or any defect or irregularity in any election of any
particular options or for any particular option holder, provided that if we
grant any such waiver, it will be granted for all option holders and options
for which elections have been made.&#160; No
elections will be deemed to have been properly made until all defects or
irregularities have been cured by the option holder or waived by us.&#160; Neither we nor any other person is obligated
to give notice of any defects or irregularities in elections, nor will anyone
incur any liability for failure to give any notice.&#160; This is a one-time offer.&#160; We will strictly enforce the election period,
subject only to an extension that we may grant in our discretion.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Important: The election form together
with all other required documents must be received by Apple via fax at (408)&nbsp;253-7457,
on or before 5:00 p.m., Pacific Time, on Monday, April 16, 2007.</font></b></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-72.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">8.</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Additional
Documents to Read.</b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">You should be sure to
read the Offer to Amend and all documents referenced therein before deciding to
participate in the offer.</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-72.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">9.</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Important
Tax Information.</b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">You should refer to
Section 14 of the Offer to Amend, if applicable, which contains important U.S.
federal and non-U.S. income tax information.&#160;
<b><i style="font-weight:bold;">We also recommend that you consult with a
financial, legal and/or tax planner regarding the personal tax consequences of
this offer to you before deciding whether or not to participate in this offer.</i></b>&#160; You should direct general questions about the
terms of this offer or requests for general tax information about this offer to
stockquestions@apple.com or contact Sheri Parker at 408-974-2683.</font></p>

<p align="right" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:right;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Exhibit
(a)(1)(D)</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">COMPLETE AND RETURN THIS FORM
ONLY IF YOU HAVE<br>
CHANGED YOUR MIND AND YOU DO NOT WANT TO AMEND SOME OR ALL OF <br>
YOUR ELIGIBLE OPTIONS</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">APPLE INC.</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">OFFER TO AMEND THE EXERCISE PRICE
OF CERTAIN OPTIONS<br>
<u>WITHDRAWAL FORM</u></font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">You previously received
(1) the Offer to Amend the Exercise Price of Certain Options (the &#147;Offer to
Amend&#148;); (2) the Email to All Eligible Option Holders; (3) the Election Form;
(4) and this Withdrawal Form. You signed and returned the election form, in
which you elected to ACCEPT Apple&#146;s offer for some or all of your eligible
options.&#160; You should submit this form
only if you now wish to change that election and REJECT Apple&#146;s offer for some
or all of your eligible options.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">To withdraw your election
to accept the offer for some or all of your eligible options, you must sign,
date and deliver this withdrawal form via facsimile at (408) 253-7457 on or
before 5:00 p.m., Pacific Time, on Monday, April 16, 2007.&#160; You should note that if you withdraw your
acceptance of the offer, you will not receive amended options in replacement
for the withdrawn options and those options will not be amended and you will
not receive any cash payments for them.&#160;
You will keep all of the options that you withdraw.&#160; These options will continue to be subject to
the terms and conditions of the Apple 1997 Employee Stock Option Plan under
which they were granted.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">You may change this
withdrawal and again elect to accept the offer for some or all of your eligible
options by faxing a new election form to (408) 253-7457 on or before 5:00 p.m.,
Pacific Time, on Monday, April 16, 2007.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Please check the
appropriate box:</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Wingdings" style="font-size:10.0pt;">o</font><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>I
wish to withdraw my election to accept the offer for all of my eligible options
and instead REJECT the offer.&#160; I do not
wish to accept the offer for any option grants.</b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">OR</font></b></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Wingdings" style="font-size:10.0pt;">o</font><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>I

listed below (and on any additional sheets which I have attached to this
form).&#160; I still wish to accept the offer
for the rest of the eligible options listed on the last properly submitted
election form.</b></p>

 <p style="margin:24.0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2</font></p> <br><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="center">

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">



<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">APPLE INC.</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">OFFER TO AMEND THE EXERCISE PRICE
OF CERTAIN OPTIONS<br>
INSTRUCTIONS TO THE WITHDRAWAL FORM</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">FORMING PART OF THE TERMS AND
CONDITIONS OF THE OFFER</font></b></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-72.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">1.</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Delivery
of Withdrawal Form.</b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A properly completed and
executed original of this withdrawal form must be received by the Company, via
facsimile at (408) 253-7457 on or before 5:00 p.m., Pacific Time, on Monday,
April 16, 2007 (referred to as the expiration of the offer).&#160; If Apple extends the offer, this withdrawal
form must be received by the Company via fax at (408) 253-7457 by the date and
time of the extended expiration of the offer.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The delivery of all
required documents, including withdrawal forms and any new election forms, is
at your risk.&#160; Delivery will be deemed
made only when actually received via fax by the Company.&#160; In all cases, you should allow sufficient
time to ensure timely delivery.&#160; Apple
intends to confirm the receipt of your withdrawal form by email within two U.S.
business days; if you have not received such an email confirmation of receipt,
it is your responsibility to ensure that your withdrawal form has been received
by the Company.&#160; Only responses that are
complete, signed and actually received by the Company by the deadline will be
accepted.&#160; Responses may only be
submitted via fax. &#160;Responses submitted
by any other means, including hand delivery, email, United States mail (or
other post) and Federal Express (or similar delivery service), are not
permitted.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">You should note that any
options for which you previously elected to accept this offer, but did not
withdraw from the offer, will remain bound by your prior election form.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Although by submitting a withdrawal form you have
withdrawn from the offer some or all the options for which you previously chose
to accept the offer, you may change your mind and re-elect to accept the offer
for the withdrawn options until the expiration of the offer.&#160; You should note that you may not rescind any
withdrawal and any eligible options withdrawn will be deemed not to have had
proper elections made for purposes of the offer, unless you properly re-elect
to amend those options before the expiration of the offer.&#160; Re-elections for options may be made at any
time before the expiration of the offer.&#160;
If Apple extends the offer beyond that time, you may re-elect for your
options at any time until the extended expiration of the offer.&#160; To re-elect for some or all of the withdrawn
options, you must fax a later dated and signed election form with the required
information to (408) 253-7457 while you still have the right to participate in
the offer.&#160; You will not be deemed to
have made a proper election for your options for purposes of the offer unless
you fax, prior to the expiration of the offer, a new election form following
the procedures described in the instructions to the election form.&#160; This new election form must be signed and
dated after your original election form and any withdrawal form you have
submitted.&#160; Upon the receipt of such a
new, properly filled out, signed and dated election form, any previously
submitted election form or withdrawal form will be disregarded and will be
considered replaced in full by the new election form.&#160; You will be bound by the last properly
submitted election or withdrawal form received by us prior to the expiration of
the offer.</font></p>


 <p style="margin:24.0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3</font></p> <br><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="center">

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">



<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Apple intends to confirm the receipt of your election
form and/or any withdrawal form by email within two U.S. business days.&#160; If you have not received an email
confirmation that Apple has received your response, you must confirm that we
have received your election form and/or any withdrawal form.&#160; If you need to confirm receipt after two U.S.
business days have elapsed, you may email stockquestions@apple.com or contact
Sheri Parker at 408-974-2683.&#160; Although
it is Apple&#146;s intent to send you an email confirmation of receipt of this
withdrawal form, by signing this withdrawal form, you waive any right to
receive any notice of the withdrawal of your election to amend your options.</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-72.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">2.</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Signatures
on this Withdrawal Form.</b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">If this withdrawal form
is signed by the holder of the eligible options, the signature must correspond
with the name as written on the face of the option agreement or agreements to
which the options are subject without alteration, enlargement or any change
whatsoever.&#160; If your name has been
legally changed since your option agreement was signed, please submit proof of
the legal name change.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">If this withdrawal form
is signed by a trustee, executor, administrator, guardian, attorney-in-fact,
officer of a corporation or other person acting in a fiduciary or
representative capacity, that person should so indicate when signing, and
proper evidence satisfactory to Apple of the authority of that person to act on
your behalf must be submitted with this withdrawal form.</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-72.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">3.</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Other
Information on this Withdrawal Form.</b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In addition to signing
this withdrawal form, you must print your name and employee number, if any, and
indicate the date and time at which you signed.&#160;
You must also include your current corporate email address, or if no
corporate email address is applicable, then a current email address at which
you can be contacted.</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-72.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">4.</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Requests
for Assistance or Additional Copies.</b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">If you have any questions
or requests for assistance, as well as requests for additional copies of the
Offer to Amend, the election form or this withdrawal form please email
stockquestions@apple.com or contact Sheri Parker at 408-974-2683.&#160; Copies will be furnished promptly at Apple&#146;s
expense.</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-72.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">5.</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Irregularities.</b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We will determine, in our
discretion, all questions as to the form of documents and the validity, form,
eligibility (including time of receipt) and acceptance of any withdrawal
forms.&#160; Our determination of these
matters will be final and binding on all parties.&#160; We reserve the right to reject any withdrawal
forms that we determine are not in good order or that we determine are unlawful
to accept.&#160; We also reserve the right to
waive any of the conditions of the offer or any defect or irregularity in any
withdrawal form or for any particular option holder, provided that if we grant
any such waiver, it will be granted for all option holders and options for
which elections have been made.&#160; No
withdrawal of options will be deemed to have been properly made until all
defects or irregularities have been cured by the withdrawing option holder or
waived by us.&#160; Neither we nor any other
person is obligated to give notice of any defects or irregularities in </font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">elections, nor will
anyone incur any liability for failure to give any notice.&#160; This is a one-time offer, and we will
strictly enforce the election period, subject only to an extension that we may
grant in our discretion.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:0pt;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Important:
The withdrawal form together with all other required documents must be received

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-72.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">6.</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Additional

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">You should be sure to
read the Offer to Amend and all documents referenced therein, before making any
decisions regarding participation in, or withdrawal from, the offer.</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt 72.0pt;text-indent:-72.0pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">7.</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Important

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">You should refer to

of this offer or requests for general tax information about this offer, please
email stockquestions@apple.com or contact Sheri Parker at 408-974-2683.</font></p>

<p align="right" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:right;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Exhibit
(a)(1)(F)</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">FORM OF AMENDMENT TO STOCK OPTION
AGREEMENT AND<br>
PROMISE TO MAKE CASH PAYMENT</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">To:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">From:&#160; Apple
Inc.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Date:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Subject:&#160;
Amendment of Your Stock Options</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">You have elected to participate in the Offer to Amend
the Exercise Price of Certain Options to have the exercise price of certain of
your options amended.&#160; We have accepted
your election to amend the options listed on the attached Schedule of Amended
Options and Cash Payments (the &#147;Options&#148;).&#160;
These Options are now exercisable, subject to vesting and the other
terms thereof, at the amended exercise price as listed on the attached Schedule
of Amended Options and Cash Payments.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In exchange for your agreement to amend your options
to purchase shares of Apple Inc. common stock, as indicated by your election
form, Apple Inc. hereby promises to pay you a cash payment for them as
described on the Schedule of Amended Options and Cash Payments attached hereto.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Any such payment will be paid, less applicable tax
withholding, promptly on or after January 25, 2008.&#160; The payments due to you are shown on the
attached Schedule of Amended Options and Cash Payments.&#160; These payments are not subject to vesting.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This memo acts as an amendment to each of your
Options.&#160; To the extent not amended by
this memo, your Options will continue to be subject to the terms and conditions
of the Apple Inc. 1997 Employee Stock Option Plan under which the original
options were granted.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This memo is subject to the terms and conditions of
the offer as set forth in: (1) the Offer to Amend the Exercise Price of Certain
Options; (2) the Email to All Eligible Option Holders; (3) the Election Form;
and (4) the Withdrawal Form (collectively, the &#147;Offer Documents&#148;), all of which
are incorporated herein by reference.&#160;
This memo and the Offer Documents reflect the entire agreement between
you and Apple concerning this transaction.&#160;
This memo may be amended only by means of a writing signed by you and an
authorized officer of Apple.</font></p>

<p align="right" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:right;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Exhibit
(a)(1)(G)</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">FORMS OF CONFIRMATION EMAILS</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:24.0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:center;text-indent:0pt;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Confirmation Email to Option Holders who Elect to Participate<br>
in the Offer to Amend the Exercise Price of Certain Options</font></i></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Apple Inc. has received your election form dated &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;,
2007, by which you elected to have some or all of your outstanding eligible
options amended in accordance with the terms of the Offer to Amend.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">If you change your mind, you may withdraw your
election as to some or all of your eligible options by completing and signing
the withdrawal form that was previously provided to you, and faxing it to (408)
253-7457 no later than 5:00 p.m., Pacific Time, on Monday, April 16, 2007.&#160; Only withdrawal forms that are complete,
signed and actually received via fax by Apple by the deadline will be
accepted.&#160; Withdrawal forms submitted by
hand delivery, email, United States mail (or other post) and Federal Express
(or similar delivery service) are not permitted.&#160; If you have questions concerning the
submission of your form, please email stockquestions@apple.com or contact Sheri
Parker at 408-974-2683.&#160; Please note that
our receipt of your election form is not by itself an acceptance of the
options.&#160; For purposes of the offer,
Apple will be deemed to have accepted options for which proper elections have
been made and not properly withdrawn as of the date when Apple gives oral or
written notice to the option holders generally of its acceptance of such
options, which notice may be made by press release, email or other method of
communication. &#160;Apple&#146;s formal acceptance
is expected to take place shortly after the end of the offer period.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:24.0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:center;text-indent:0pt;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Confirmation Email to Option Holders who Withdraw their Stock Options<br>
from the Offer to Amend the Exercise Price of Certain Stock Options</font></i></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Apple Inc. has received your withdrawal form dated &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;,
2007, by which you rejected Apple&#146;s offer to amend some or all of your
outstanding eligible options.&#160; <b><i style="font-weight:bold;">Any options you have not withdrawn will remain
bound pursuant to your prior election form.</i></b></font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">If you change your mind, you may once again elect to
accept the offer for some or all of your eligible options by completing and
submitting a new election form and faxing it to (408) 753-7457 no later than
5:00 p.m., Pacific Time, on Monday, April 16, 2007.&#160; If you have questions concerning the
submission of your form, please email stockquestions@apple.com or contact Sheri
Parker at 408-974-2683.</font></p>

<TYPE>EX-99.(A)(1)(H)

<body lang="EN-US">

<div>


<p align="right" style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:right;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Exhibit
(a)(1)(H)</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">FORM OF INITIAL REMINDER EMAIL TO
ELIGIBLE OPTION HOLDERS</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As outlined in an email dated March 16, 2007, and in
the documents included with that email, Internal Revenue Code Section 409A
imposes certain adverse tax consequences (including recognition of taxable
ordinary income at vesting, an additional 20% penalty tax and interest charges)
on stock options that (i) had an original exercise price per share that was
less than the fair market value per share of the common stock underlying the option
on the date the grant was actually finalized <u>and</u> (ii) that vest <u>after</u>
December 31, 2004.&#160; The Section 409A
taxes are in addition to ordinary income taxes on stock option gains that are
reported on your 2006 W-2 Form.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">You are receiving this email because our records
indicate that some of your Apple stock options are or will be affected by
Section 409A. Apple has offered you, through a &#147;Tender Offer&#148;, the opportunity
to avoid the Section 409A tax consequences on your affected stock options by
amending the exercise price of such options and receiving cash payments.&#160; Note that if you wish to participate in the
Tender Offer and avoid the Section 409A impact, you will need to fill out,
sign, and date the Election Form attached to the March 16, 2007 email. The
Election Form must be received by Apple via fax at (408) 253-7457 <b><u style="font-weight:bold;">no later than 5:00 p.m., Pacific Time, on Monday,
April 16, 2007.</u></b> However, participation in this offer is
completely voluntary.&#160; You are not
required to accept this offer.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">All of the details of Apple&#146;s offer to you are
included in the email dated March 16, 2007 and the attachments to the email.&nbsp;&nbsp;For
more information on how to participate in the offer, you may email
stockquestions@apple.com or contact Sheri Parker at 408-974-2683.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">FORM OF ADDITIONAL REMINDER EMAIL
TO ELIGIBLE OPTION HOLDERS</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Internal Revenue Code Section 409A imposes certain
adverse tax consequences (including recognition of taxable ordinary income at
vesting, an additional 20% penalty tax and interest charges) on stock options
that (i) had an original exercise price per share that was less than the fair
market value per share of the common stock underlying the option on the date
the grant was actually finalized<u> and</u> (ii) that vest <u>after</u>
December 31, 2004.&#160; The Section 409A taxes
are in addition to ordinary income taxes on stock option gains that are
reported on your 2006 W-2 Form.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">You are receiving this email because our records
indicate that some of your Apple stock options are or will be affected by
Section 409A.&#160; Apple has offered you,
through a &#147;Tender Offer&#148;, the opportunity to avoid the Section 409A tax
consequences on your affected stock options by amending the exercise price of
such options and receiving cash payments.&#160;
Note that if you wish to participate in the Tender Offer and avoid the
Section 409A impact, you will need to fill out, sign, and date the Election
Form attached to the March 16, 2007 email. The Election Form must be received
by Apple via fax at (408) 253-7457 <b><u style="font-weight:bold;">no later than 5:00 p.m.,
Pacific Time, on Monday, April 16, 2007.</u></b> However, participation
in this offer is completely voluntary.&#160;
You are not required to accept this offer.</font></p>
