<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">All of the details of Apple&#146;s offer to you are
included in the email dated March 16, 2007 and the attachments to the email.&nbsp;&nbsp;For
more information on how to participate in the offer, you may email
stockquestions@apple.com or contact Sheri Parker at 408-974-2683.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">FORM OF ADDITIONAL REMINDER EMAIL
TO ELIGIBLE OPTION HOLDERS WHO <br>
HAVE NOT RESPONDED TO THE OFFER</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As outlined in an email dated March 16, 2007, and in
the documents included with that email, Internal Revenue Code Section 409A
imposes certain adverse tax consequences (including recognition of taxable
ordinary income at vesting, an additional 20% penalty tax and interest charges)
on stock options that (i) had an original exercise price per share that was
less than the fair market value per share of the common stock underlying the
option on the date the grant was actually finalized <u>and</u> (ii) that vest <u>after</u>
December 31, 2004.&#160; The Section 409A
taxes are in addition to ordinary income taxes on stock option gains that are
reported on your 2006 W-2 Form.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Apple has offered you, through a &#147;Tender Offer&#148;, the
opportunity to avoid the Section 409A tax consequences on your affected stock
options by amending the exercise price of such options and receiving cash
payments.&#160; <b>You are
receiving this email because Apple has not received any communication from you
regarding whether you wish to elect to participate in this offer.</b></font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Note that if you wish to participate in the Tender
Offer and avoid the Section 409A impact, you will need to fill out, sign, and
date the Election Form attached to the March 16, 2007 email. The Election Form
must be received by Apple via fax at (408) 253-7457 <b><u style="font-weight:bold;">no later
than 5:00 p.m., Pacific Time, on Monday, April 16, 2007.</u></b>
However, participation in this offer is completely voluntary.&#160; You are not required to accept this offer.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">All of the details of Apple&#146;s offer to you are
included in the email dated March 16, 2007 and the attachments to the email.&nbsp;&nbsp;For
more information on how to participate in the offer, you may email
stockquestions@apple.com or contact Sheri Parker at 408-974-2683.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">FORM OF FINAL REMINDER EMAIL TO
ELIGIBLE OPTION HOLDERS WHO <br>
HAVE NOT RESPONDED TO THE OFFER</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Subject: <b>&#160;FINAL NOTICE: ACTION REQUIRED -&#160; Section 409A Income Tax Liability</b></font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As of today, we have not yet received your Election
Form to adopt the tender offer solution that has been designed to protect
certain of your stock options from substantial tax penalties under Section 409A
of the Internal Revenue Code. This will be the final reminder of your ability
to participate in this offer.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As outlined in an email dated March 16, 2007, and in
the documents included with that email, Internal Revenue Code Section 409A
imposes certain adverse tax consequences (including recognition of taxable
ordinary income at vesting, an additional 20% penalty tax and interest charges)
on stock options that (i) had an original exercise price per share that was
less than the fair market value per share of the common stock underlying the
option on the date the grant was actually finalized <u>and</u> (ii) that vest <u>after</u>
December 31, 2004.&#160; The Section 409A
taxes </font></p>


 <p style="margin:24.0pt 0pt .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2</font></p> <br><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="center">

<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='2',FILE='C:\fc\7481522722_D11850_1870758\8219-1-li.htm',USER='jmsproofassembler',CD='Mar 15 08:15 2007' -->
<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">



<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">are in addition to ordinary income taxes on stock
option gains that are reported on your 2006 W-2 Form.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">If you wish to participate in the Tender Offer and
avoid the Section 409A impact, you will need to fill out, sign, and date the
Election Form attached to the March 16, 2007 email. The Election Form must be
received by Apple via fax at (408) 253-7457 <b><u style="font-weight:bold;">no later
than 5:00 p.m., Pacific Time, on Monday, April 16, 2007.</u></b>&#160; We have also attached a copy of Election Form
to this email for your convenience.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12.0pt;text-indent:36.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">If you do not fax to Apple your completed Election
Form by the deadline, you will likely be subject to the Section 409A tax
consequences described above and in the documents attached to the March 16,
2007 email and the documents attached to that email.</font></p>
